This bike is easily the best MTB I've ridden so far https://www.youtube.com/post/UgkxHL1v1R3NE5x4KiYfyt8dnQmyNYz7qi5L   Assembly was pretty self explanatory. To be fair though, I immediately swapped the derailleurs for some smoother Shimanos and thumb shifters instead of the stock twist shifters. The sheer size of this bike dwarfs most 26" bikes of the same class. I'm only 5'8" but I can sit comfortably with the saddle and suspension adjusted properly, even though my feet can just barely touch the ground. A small price to pay for such a beast. I love that Mongoose included TOOLLESS WHEELS, it makes transporting and techwork so much easier. The aluminum frame makes it so much lighter than I expected. In comparison, mine weighs only 2lbs more than the 24" my friend rides. I'm not the most in shape rider but even I can climb inclines like a breeze with this bike and it's massive wheels and 21 speeds.

My opinion would not be pleasant to read, but I definitely should still say, cause that's what comments are for, right? So This video is pretty weak. Now let me explain. When I was watching, I constantly felt that something was missing... Then I re-watched the urban freeride from Paris and... You immediately can see the difference! That video actually feels dynamic! There was some kind of a story, it feels that you actually rolling somewhere. Much more dynamic picture, much more different interesting shots. Fabio's riding skills did not got worse (obviously), but the quality of this video definitely is much worse. In this Chili video you: 1. Spoiled all the fun stuff at the first second 2. No story, just a cut of random shots from random locations and you show me the same jump 3 times in a row, come on.. 3. Much much less shots, video doesn't feels dynamic and alive. More shots from the helmet needed. 4. You don't even try to hide ramps anymore, like you did before! This suppose to be urban, isn't it? Those are easy to see exact points, that I spot as a regular viewer. Guys, I love you, I'm a fan! Don't know what happened with you, but... This video you did not nailed at all. Still a great video, but compared to your other works, it feels kinda lame...
